***несмотря.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> (1001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesmotrjá na</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>in spite of, despite <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the action must be completed in advance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:серьезный.html>серьёзную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:наконец.html>наконе́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:врач.html>врачи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вылечить.html>вы́лечили</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nesmotrjá na</b> serʹjóznuju boléznʹ, nakonéc vračí výlečili menjá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Despite</b> the bad illness, the doctors finally cured me.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несмотря.html>несмотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положительный.html>положи́тельную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обстановка.html>обстано́вку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:конференция.html>конфере́нция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закончиться.html>зако́нчилась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бедствие.html>бе́дствием</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nesmotrjá na</b> položítelʹnuju obstanóvku, konferéncija zakónčilasʹ bédstvijem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Despite</b> the positive atmosphere, the conference ended with a disaster.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>notwithstanding</li>
<li>although</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несоблюдение.html>несоблюде́ние</a> (31156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobljudénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоблюдение.html>несоблюде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesobljudénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоблюдение.html>несоблюде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоблюдение.html>несоблюде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоблюдение.html>несоблюде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>noncompliance</li>
<li>nonobservance</li>
<li>infraction, violation</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несокрушимый.html>несокруши́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesokrušímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>indestructible, invincible, unconquerable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несокрушимый.html>несокруши́мая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesokrušímaja</b> vólja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">iron will</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ши́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мый</b>

***несоответствие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствие</a> (13542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesootvétstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>discrepancy, disparity, lack of correspondence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:характер.html>хара́ктеров</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesootvétstvije</b> xarákterov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">incompatibility of temperaments</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельный.html>несостоя́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nesostojátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesostojátelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>insolvency, failure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объявить.html>объяви́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:несостоятельность.html>несостоя́тельности</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obʺjavítʹ o <b>nesostojátelʹnosti</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">declare bankruptcy</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>modest means</li>
<li>unfoundedness, groundlessness, flimsiness, unsoundness</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несправедливость.html>несправедли́вость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nespravedlívostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несправедливость.html>несправедли́вости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несправедливость.html>несправедли́вости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несправедливость.html>несправедли́востей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несравненный.html>несравне́нный</a> (15897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сравнить.html>сравни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sravnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несравненный.html>несравне́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesravnénnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> incomparable, matchless, unmatched, peerless</li></ol>

<ol><li>unbearably
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  “хори́стка  | The Chorus Girl | ”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> |  republished in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>Русский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></cite>, 2002:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимо.html>нестерпи́мо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жаркий.html>жа́рко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душный.html>ду́шно</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Býlo <b>nesterpímo</b> žárko i dúšno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It was <b>unbearably</b> hot and stifling.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестерпимый.html>нестерпи́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nesterpímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***нести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a> (871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nestì</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понести.html>понести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bear, to bring, to carry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумка.html>су́мки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nestí</b> tjažólyje súmki</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to carry</b> heavy bags</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to carry, to bear, to support
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>должны́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответственность.html>отве́тственность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní dolžný <b>nestí</b> otvétstvennostʹ za ošíbki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">They need <b>to bear</b> responsibility for the mistakes.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lay (eggs)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снести.html>снести́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk (about), to babble on (about)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздор.html>вздор</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несёт</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što (za vzdor) on <b>nesjót</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what (utter) nonsense he is talking!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несёт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne ponimáju, što oná tam <b>nesjót</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have no idea what she is babbling on about</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be carried away, to go over the limits
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1931</b>,  Ильф <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Петров (Ilf and Petrov),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%97%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Золотой телёнок"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>Золото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теленок.html>телёнок</a></a></cite>  | <cite>The Little Golden Calf</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— росси́я <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забу́дет</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:рявкнуть.html>ря́вкнул</a> Остап. Ипполит Матвеевич, <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сладкий.html>сла́дкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пирожок.html>пирожо́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоумение.html>недоуме́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шал</a> Остапа, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несло́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>Вели́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комбинатор.html>комбина́тор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствовал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдохновение.html>вдохнове́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:упоительный.html>упои́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> вышесредним <a href = vnd.unilang:шантаж.html>шантажо́м</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройтись.html>прошёлся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:барс.html>барс</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Rossíja vas ne zabúdet! — rjávknul Ostap. Ippolit Matvejevič, deržá v ruké sládkij pirožók, s nedouménijem slúšal Ostapa, no uderžátʹ jevó býlo nelʹzjá. Jevó <b>nesló</b>. Velikij kombinátor čúvstvoval vdoxnovénije, upoítelʹnoje sostojánije pered vyšesrednim šantažóm. On prošelsja po kómnate, kak bars.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Russia will never forget you!" bellowed Ostap. Ippolit Matveyevich, holding a sweet bun in his hand, listened to Ostap in perplexity but was unable to hold him. He was <b>carried away</b>. The great combinator felt inspiration, ravishing condition before the upper-middle class blackmailing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1931</b>,  Ильф <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Петров (Ilf and Petrov),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%97%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BB%D1%91%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Золотой телёнок"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>Золото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теленок.html>телёнок</a></a></cite>  | <cite>The Little Golden Calf</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Остап <a href = vnd.unilang:отогнать.html>отогна́л</a> Полесова <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> Никеши <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Влади <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неподдельный.html>неподде́льной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровость.html>суро́востью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́л</a>:<br /> — <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полок.html>полку́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́ли</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>Придётся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:послужить.html>послужи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отечество.html>оте́честву</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дворянин.html>дворя́не</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>О́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:запад.html>за́пад</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>помо́жет</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:крепиться.html>крепи́тесь</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вкла́дов</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ции</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a>. <br />Остапа <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>несло́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>Дело</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:налаживаться.html>нала́живалось</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ostap otognál Polesova ot Nikeši i Vladi i s nepoddélʹnoj suróvostʹju sprosíl:<br /> — V kakóm polku služíli? Pridetsja poslužítʹ otéčestvu. Vy dvorjáne? Očenʹ xorošó. Západ nam pomóžet. Krepítesʹ. Pólnaja tájna vkládov, to jestʹ organizácii. Vnimánije. <br />Ostapa <b>nesló</b>. Delo kak búdto naláživalosʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Ostap drove Polesov away from Mikesha and Vladya and asked with genuine harshness: "In which regiment did you serve? You'll have to serve your motherland. Are you noblemen? Very well. The West is going to help us. Hold on. Full secrecy of accounts, I mean, organization. Attention." Ostap got <b>carried away</b>. The business seemed to go smoothly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>Нести́</a></b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:понести.html>понести́</a> are concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нёс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-нес-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***нестись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a> (2977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронестись.html>пронести́сь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:донестись.html>донести́сь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">снести́сь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurtle, to dash, to race, to tear, to scurry <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to move rapidly, violently, or without control</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to come, <i>(sound)</i> to reach one's ears, to be heard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>несётся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запах.html>за́пах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гарь.html>га́ри</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz okná <b>nesjótsja</b> zápax gári</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">there's the smell of burning coming from the window</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lay eggs
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">снести́сь</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a></b> is a concrete verb. The counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носиться.html>носи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нёс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́сь</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — снестись.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-нес-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b>; постфикс: <b>-сь</b>.
</p>
